VERSION=V1.6.0

[V1.0.0] 2025-08-10
奠基版本发布
- 核心工具集：发布了基础 Python 脚本工具包。
- 基础功能：支持 SKU 销量统计、库存上传以及基础交易数据的清洗与处理。

[V1.1.0] 2025-09-28
财务模块集成
- 多源数据集成：集成了 Order Earning 资金流数据源，实现了业财一体化。
- 逻辑优化：在交易处理逻辑中引入了基于哈希 (Hash) 的去重算法，提升了数据处理的准确性。
- 报表系统：发布了多维度的盈亏分析报表体系。

[V1.2.0] 2025-11-29
智能化运维模块
- 机器学习集成：集成了 K-Means 聚类和 PCA 降维算法，实现了 SKU 的自动化打标与分层。
- 高级分析工具：新增了 Listing 流量诊断工具与 Combo 组合策略评估模型。

[V1.3.0] 2025-12-02
Web 应用化转型
- UI/UX 全面升级：从命令行脚本迁移至 Streamlit Web 框架，实现了交互式可视化操作界面。
- CRM 客户管理模块：引入了基于 RFM (最近一次消费、消费频率、消费金额) 模型的客户价值分析功能，支持精准用户画像。

[V1.4.0] 2025-12-04
企业级架构重构
- 自动化 ETL 流水线：发布了覆盖数据加载 (Ingest)、解析 (Parsing)、转换 (Transformation) 和归档 (Archiving) 的全生命周期自动化处理流程。
- 灾难恢复系统：引入了具备时间点恢复能力的数据库备份与还原中心 (Backup & Restore Center)。
- 基础设施升级：实现了配置与代码的完全分离 (Configuration Decoupling)；前端架构全面迁移至组件化 UI 模式 (Component-Based UI)。

[V1.4.1] 2025-12-05
核心数据完整性与算法热修复
- ETL 智能去重 (Smart Upsert)：实施了基于时间窗口剪枝和四维复合主键 (Seller + Order + Item + Action) 匹配的分区去重策略，实现了毫秒级精准覆盖，彻底消除了误删历史数据的风险。
- 全链路归一化 (Global Normalization)：在所有分析器 (Sales, Profit, Ordering, Prediction) 中强制实施严格的 SKU 归一化标准（大写/去空格），解决了报表首列重复和统计偏差问题。
- 数据流加固 (Data Pipeline Hardening)：修复了 Repository 到 Analyzer 传输过程中的静默数据丢失问题；增强了数据仓库中日期格式解析的容错能力。
- Bug 修复：修正了销量统计分析中店铺分桶统计丢失的问题，并补全了智能补货计划中的状态备注字段。

[V1.5.0] 2025-12-05
企业级安全架构与性能革命
- 企业级安全架构 (Enterprise Security Architecture)：实施了 PBKDF2-SHA256 密码加密存储与防暴力破解策略；敏感操作引入“操作密码+确认短语”双重校验机制，全面提升系统安全性。
- 高性能 ETL 引擎 (High-Performance ETL Engine)：核心转换逻辑升级为 Pandas 向量化矩阵运算，摒弃低效循环，处理速度提升 20-50 倍；引入 Staging Table 原子写入策略，确保多店铺数据并发上传时的绝对一致性。
- 深度审计系统 (Deep Audit System)：发布了显微镜级业务审计日志，支持数据变更的“修改前 vs 修改后”逐字段比对，实现全链路操作可追溯。
- 用户权限与运维增强 (User Access & Ops Enhancement)：构建了基于 RBAC 的细粒度权限控制体系，支持针对 ETL、报表等模块的独立鉴权；新增数据库运维“危险区域”，支持一键重置测试环境（仅清空流水，保留用户与基础档案）。

[V1.6.0] 2025-12-10
分布式并发架构与安全权限重塑 (Distributed Concurrency & Security Governance)
用户权限模型重设计 (RBAC Redesign)：
- 在原有的粗粒度 RBAC 基础上，全面升级了对 模块、Tab 页面及操作动作 的三级授权设计。
- 这一设计允许管理员精确配置用户对核心功能如 ETL、报表等模块的访问权限，实现了真正的 最小权限原则。
分布式并发控制架构 (Distributed Concurrency Control)：
- 架构核心引入了基于数据库持久化的 分布式锁管理器 (LockManager) 。
- 对 ETL 交易数据导入、库存同步 和 SKU 档案维护 等核心写入资源实施了严格的互斥锁机制 。
会话级安全回滚机制 (Session-Level Safety Rollback)：
- 系统现在深度绑定了会话生命周期与数据完整性 。
- 一旦检测到用户在 ETL 流程中途异常退出或强制登出，系统将自动检查并释放其持有的锁，并立即触发 Data_Transaction 脏数据回滚 (Auto-Rollback) 程序，清空原始表中的未提交数据，防止数据污染 。
日志系统深度强化（Deep Audit System Update）：
- 日志记录已全面优化，确保每个操作日志均包含完整的 操作人、操作动作、目标表名以及来源 IP 等溯源信息 。
- 审计日志现在具备更强的鲁棒性，即使在多线程/多进程环境下，也能通过 ContextFilter 准确捕获当前操作用户的会话信息 。

==================== START FILE: stop_server.sh ====================
#!/bin/bash

# ========================================================
# Eaglestar ERP - macOS 关闭脚本 (全栈清理)
# ========================================================

BASE_DIR="$( cd "$( dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}" )" &> /dev/null && pwd )"
cd "$BASE_DIR"

SERVER_PID_FILE="$BASE_DIR/server.pid"
TUNNEL_PID_FILE="$BASE_DIR/tunnel.pid"

echo "🛑 正在停止服务..."

# 1. 关闭 Streamlit 主程序
if [ -f "$SERVER_PID_FILE" ]; then
    PID=$(cat "$SERVER_PID_FILE")
    if ps -p $PID > /dev/null; then
        kill $PID
        echo " 已终止 ERP 主进程 (PID: $PID)"
        rm "$SERVER_PID_FILE"
    else
        echo "⚠️  ERP 进程已不存在，清理 PID 文件。"
        rm "$SERVER_PID_FILE"
    fi
else
    echo "️  未找到 ERP PID 文件。"
fi

# 2. 关闭 Cloudflare Tunnel
if [ -f "$TUNNEL_PID_FILE" ]; then
    PID=$(cat "$TUNNEL_PID_FILE")
    if ps -p $PID > /dev/null; then
        kill $PID
        echo " 已终止 Cloudflare Tunnel (PID: $PID)"
        rm "$TUNNEL_PID_FILE"
    else
        echo "⚠️  Tunnel 进程已不存在，清理 PID 文件。"
        rm "$TUNNEL_PID_FILE"
    fi
else
    echo "️  未找到 Tunnel PID 文件。"
fi

# 3. 兜底清理 (防止进程残留)
# 清理 Streamlit
LEFTOVER_ST=$(pgrep -f "streamlit run app.py")
if [ -n "$LEFTOVER_ST" ]; then
    echo "🧹 清理残留的 Streamlit 进程..."
    echo "$LEFTOVER_ST" | xargs kill
fi

# 清理 Cloudflare (只清理带 token 参数的进程，防止误杀其他 tunnel)
LEFTOVER_CF=$(pgrep -f "cloudflared tunnel run --token")
if [ -n "$LEFTOVER_CF" ]; then
    echo "🧹 清理残留的 Cloudflare 进程..."
    echo "$LEFTOVER_CF" | xargs kill
fi

echo "😴 防休眠模式已解除，服务已全部关闭。"
==================== END FILE: stop_server.sh ====================

==================== START FILE: start_server.sh ====================
#!/bin/bash

# ========================================================
# Eaglestar ERP - macOS 启动脚本 (含 Cloudflare Tunnel)
# ========================================================

# 1. 确保进入脚本所在的目录 (项目根目录)
BASE_DIR="$( cd "$( dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}" )" &> /dev/null && pwd )"
cd "$BASE_DIR"

# --- 配置区域 ---
SERVER_PID_FILE="$BASE_DIR/server.pid"
TUNNEL_PID_FILE="$BASE_DIR/tunnel.pid"
LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/logs"
SERVER_LOG="$LOG_DIR/server_runtime.log"
TUNNEL_LOG="$LOG_DIR/cloudflared.log"

# Cloudflare Token
CF_TOKEN="YOUR_CF_TOKEN_HERE"

# 确保日志目录存在
mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"

# 2. 环境检查与清理
if [ -f "$SERVER_PID_FILE" ]; then
    PID=$(cat "$SERVER_PID_FILE")
    if ps -p $PID > /dev/null; then
        echo " 服务器已经在运行中 (PID: $PID)"
        exit 1
    else
        rm "$SERVER_PID_FILE"
    fi
fi

# 3. 激活 Python 环境
echo "🚀 正在初始化环境..."
if [ -d ".venv" ]; then
    echo "🟢 激活虚拟环境 (.venv)..."
    source .venv/bin/activate
elif [ -d "venv" ]; then
    echo "🟢 激活虚拟环境 (venv)..."
    source venv/bin/activate
fi

# 4. 启动 Cloudflare Tunnel (后台运行)
echo "🌐 正在启动 Cloudflare Tunnel..."
# 使用 nohup 后台运行，日志输出到 logs/cloudflared.log
nohup cloudflared tunnel run --token $CF_TOKEN > "$TUNNEL_LOG" 2>&1 &
TUNNEL_PID=$!
echo $TUNNEL_PID > "$TUNNEL_PID_FILE"
echo "   -> Tunnel PID: $TUNNEL_PID"

# 5. 启动 Streamlit 服务器 (核心防休眠)
# caffeinate -ims: 只要这个命令在运行，电脑就不会休眠
echo "🛡️  正在启动 Streamlit 服务器 (已启用 macOS 防休眠守护)..."
nohup caffeinate -ims streamlit run app.py --server.port 8501 > "$SERVER_LOG" 2>&1 &
SERVER_PID=$!
echo $SERVER_PID > "$SERVER_PID_FILE"

# 6. 输出结果
echo "=================================================="
echo " 服务全栈启动成功！"
echo "   - ERP 主程序 PID: $SERVER_PID"
echo "   - Cloudflare PID: $TUNNEL_PID"
echo "--------------------------------------------------"
echo "📄 ERP 日志: logs/server_runtime.log"
echo "📄 CF  日志: logs/cloudflared.log"
echo "🔒 电脑已进入防休眠模式，您可以放心地锁屏。"
echo "=================================================="
==================== END FILE: start_server.sh ====================


==================== START FILE: debug_config.py ====================
# debug_config.py
import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from config.settings import settings

print("="*50)
print(f"🔍 调试模式: 检查配置加载")
print("="*50)

print(f"1. 项目根目录 (BASE_DIR): {settings.BASE_DIR}")
print(f"2. 配置目录 (CONFIG_DIR): {settings.CONFIG_DIR}")

json_path = settings.CONFIG_DIR / "modules.json"
print(f"3. 目标配置文件: {json_path}")

if not json_path.exists():
    print(" 错误: modules.json 文件不存在！")
else:
    print(" 文件存在。尝试读取内容...")
    try:
        with open(json_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            content = f.read()
            if not content.strip():
                print(" 错误: 文件是空的！")
            else:
                data = json.loads(content)
                print(f" JSON 解析成功！共找到 {len(data)} 个模块配置。")
                print("-" * 20)
                for mod in data:
                    print(f"   - [{mod.get('key')}] {mod.get('name')} (Perm: {mod.get('permission')})")
    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
        print(f" JSON 格式错误: {e}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f" 读取错误: {e}")

print("="*50)
==================== END FILE: debug_config.py ====================

==================== START FILE: app.py ====================
# app.py
"""
文件说明: Streamlit 应用入口 (Entry Point)
主要功能:
1. 配置 Streamlit 页面基础属性 (Title, Layout)。
2. 初始化认证服务 (Bootstrap Database)。
3. [New] 初始化并发锁管理器。
4. 实例化并启动动态路由引擎 (Router)。
"""

import streamlit as st
from config.settings import settings
from ui.kernel.router import Router
from core.services.auth.service import AuthService
from core.sys.lock_manager import LockManager  # [New]

# ==============================================================================
# 1. 全局配置 (必须是第一个 Streamlit 命令)
# ==============================================================================
st.set_page_config(
    page_title=settings.APP_NAME,
    page_icon="🦅",
    layout="wide",
    initial_sidebar_state="expanded",
)

# ==============================================================================
# 2. 系统初始化 (Bootstrap)
# ==============================================================================
# 确保数据库表结构存在，并创建默认账号
AuthService.initialize()

# [New] 初始化分布式锁表结构
LockManager.initialize()


# ==============================================================================
# 3. 启动路由引擎
# ==============================================================================
def main():
    """主程序入口"""
    try:
        # 实例化路由
        app_router = Router()

        # 渲染界面
        app_router.render()

    except Exception as e:
        st.error("🔥 System Critical Error (Main Loop)")
        st.exception(e)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
==================== END FILE: app.py ====================


==================== START FILE: verify_lock_system.py ====================
# verify_lock_system.py
"""
文件说明: 分布式锁系统验证脚本 (Verification Suite)
运行方式: python verify_lock_system.py
主要功能:
1. 模拟并发环境，验证 LockManager 的原子性和隔离性。
2. 验证 'Data_Transaction', 'Data_Inventory' 等关键资源的互斥逻辑。
3. 验证用户登出时的锁自动回收机制。
"""

import time
import sys
from pathlib import Path

# 添加项目根目录到 Path
project_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
sys.path.append(str(project_root))

from core.sys.lock_manager import LockManager
from core.components.db.client import DBClient


def print_step(msg):
    print(f"\n🔹 {msg}")


def print_res(success, msg):
    icon = "" if success else ""
    print(f"   {icon} {msg}")


def run_verification():
    print("🚀 开始验证分布式锁系统 (ISO/IEC 25010 Reliability Test)...")

    # 0. 初始化
    LockManager.initialize()
    RESOURCE = "Data_Test_Resource"
    USER_A = "Admin_Alice"
    USER_B = "User_Bob"

    # 清理环境
    DBClient.execute_stmt(f"DELETE FROM System_Locks WHERE resource_key='{RESOURCE}'")

    # --- Case 1: 基础互斥测试 ---
    print_step("Case 1: 互斥性测试 (Mutually Exclusive)")

    # A 获取锁
    ok, msg = LockManager.acquire_lock(RESOURCE, USER_A, "Testing Module")
    print_res(ok, f"User A 尝试加锁: {msg}")
    if not ok:
        print(" 严重错误: 初始加锁失败")
        return

    # B 尝试获取锁 (应失败)
    ok, msg = LockManager.acquire_lock(RESOURCE, USER_B, "Testing Module")
    print_res(not ok, f"User B 尝试加锁 (预期失败): {msg}")

    # --- Case 2: 锁的所有权与刷新 ---
    print_step("Case 2: 所有权验证 (Re-entrancy)")

    # A 再次获取锁 (应成功，刷新时间)
    ok, msg = LockManager.acquire_lock(RESOURCE, USER_A, "Testing Module")
    print_res(ok, f"User A 再次加锁 (刷新): {msg}")

    # --- Case 3: 正常释放流程 ---
    print_step("Case 3: 释放与抢占 (Release & Acquire)")

    # A 释放锁
    ok = LockManager.release_lock(RESOURCE, USER_A)
    print_res(ok, "User A 释放锁")

    # B 现在应该能获取锁
    ok, msg = LockManager.acquire_lock(RESOURCE, USER_B, "Testing Module")
    print_res(ok, f"User B 尝试加锁 (预期成功): {msg}")

    # --- Case 4: 强制清理 (Session Logout) ---
    print_step("Case 4: 异常中断与强制清理 (Force Release)")

    # 模拟 B 突然掉线 (Logout)，系统调用 release_all
    released_list = LockManager.release_all_user_locks(USER_B)
    print_res(RESOURCE in released_list, f"系统强制释放 User B 的锁: {released_list}")

    # A 重新获取
    ok, msg = LockManager.acquire_lock(RESOURCE, USER_A, "Testing Module")
    print_res(ok, f"User A 重新接管资源: {msg}")

    # --- 清理 ---
    LockManager.release_lock(RESOURCE, USER_A)
    print("\n🎉 验证完成: 锁管理器逻辑运行正常。")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_verification()
==================== END FILE: verify_lock_system.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/styles.py ====================
# ui/styles.py
"""
文件说明: 全局样式管理器 (Global Styles) - V3.0 Security UI
主要功能:
1. 增强 Streamlit 组件交互 (Hover 效果)。
2. [New] 安全警示样式: 为“解锁完整信息”模式提供视觉反馈。
"""

import streamlit as st


class StyleManager:
    _MAIN_STYLES = """
    <style>
        /* 1. 隐藏多余元素 */
        #MainMenu {visibility: hidden;} 
        footer {visibility: hidden;}

        /* 2. 侧边栏菜单 (Radio) */
        div[role="radiogroup"] label { 
            transition: all 0.2s cubic-bezier(0.175, 0.885, 0.32, 1.275) !important;
            border-radius: 8px;
            padding: 8px 12px !important; 
            margin-bottom: 4px; 
            border: 1px solid transparent;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        div[role="radiogroup"] label:hover { 
            transform: scale(1.05) translateX(10px) !important;
            background: rgba(78, 201, 176, 0.2) !important;
            border: 1px solid rgba(78, 201, 176, 0.5) !important; 
            box-shadow: 0 10px 25px rgba(0,0,0,0.5) !important;
            z-index: 999 !important; 
            color: #FFFFFF !important;
            font-weight: bold !important; 
        }
        div[role="radiogroup"] [aria-checked="true"] {
            color: #4EC9B0 !important;
            font-weight: 800 !important;
        }

        /* 3. Tab 标签栏 */
        button[data-baseweb="tab"] { 
            transition: all 0.2s ease-in-out !important;
            border-radius: 4px 4px 0 0 !important;
            margin: 0 4px !important; 
            border: none !important;
            border-bottom: 2px solid transparent !important;
        }
        button[data-baseweb="tab"]:hover { 
            background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.15) !important; 
            border-bottom: 3px solid #4EC9B0 !important;
            color: #FFFFFF !important; 
            transform: none !important;
        }
        button[data-baseweb="tab"][aria-selected="true"] {
            background-color: rgba(78, 201, 176, 0.25) !important;
            border-bottom: 3px solid #4EC9B0 !important;
            font-weight: bold !important;
        }

        /* 4. [New] 上帝模式警示边框 (Security Unmasked Mode) */
        @keyframes border-pulse {
            0% { border-color: rgba(255, 75, 75, 0.3); box-shadow: 0 0 10px rgba(255, 0, 0, 0.1) inset; }
            50% { border-color: rgba(255, 75, 75, 0.8); box-shadow: 0 0 30px rgba(255, 0, 0, 0.3) inset; }
            100% { border-color: rgba(255, 75, 75, 0.3); box-shadow: 0 0 10px rgba(255, 0, 0, 0.1) inset; }
        }

        .security-unmasked {
            position: fixed;
            top: 0; left: 0; width: 100vw; height: 100vh;
            border: 5px solid #FF4B4B;
            pointer-events: none; /* 让鼠标能穿透 */
            z-index: 999999;
            animation: border-pulse 2s infinite;
        }

    </style>
    """

    @classmethod
    def apply_global_styles(cls):
        """注入全局 CSS"""
        st.markdown(cls._MAIN_STYLES, unsafe_allow_html=True)

    @classmethod
    def apply_unmasked_style(cls):
        """[特权] 激活红色警示框"""
        st.markdown('<div class="security-unmasked"></div>', unsafe_allow_html=True)
==================== END FILE: ui/styles.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/components/security.py ====================
# ui/components/security.py
"""
文件说明: 安全卫士组件 (Security Gate Component) - V5.2 Four-Level Codes
主要功能:
1. [统一入口] 封装高危操作验证流程。
2. [动态策略] 支持 user, query, modify, db, system 五种令牌。
3. [智能审计] 严格判定: 仅当 (Modify + DB + System) 同时启用时，强制标记日志为不可删除。
4. [安全熔断] 连续验证失败 5 次，锁定账户并强制登出。
"""

import streamlit as st
import time
from typing import List, Tuple, Literal, Optional

from config.settings import settings
from core.services.auth.service import AuthService
from ui.kernel.session import SessionManager
from core.sys.logger import get_audit_logger
from core.services.security.policy_manager import SecurityPolicyManager

# 专用审计日志器
audit_logger = get_audit_logger()
IMMUTABLE_MARKER = "[[SECURITY_AUDIT]]"

# 定义令牌类型
TokenType = Literal["user", "query", "modify", "db", "system"]


class SecurityGate:
    """
    [安全切面] 高危操作保护器 (含熔断机制)
    """

    MAX_RETRIES = 5

    @staticmethod
    def _handle_failure(username: str, action_name: str):
        """处理验证失败逻辑: 计数 -> 报警 -> 熔断"""
        if "auth_fail_count" not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state["auth_fail_count"] = 0

        st.session_state["auth_fail_count"] += 1
        current_fails = st.session_state["auth_fail_count"]

        remaining = SecurityGate.MAX_RETRIES - current_fails

        # 记录警告日志
        audit_logger.warning(
            f"验证失败 ({current_fails}/{SecurityGate.MAX_RETRIES}) | Action: {action_name}",
            extra={"user": username, "action": "AUTH_FAIL"}
        )

        if remaining > 0:
            st.error(f" 验证失败！密码错误或权限不足。剩余尝试次数: {remaining}")
        else:
            # --- 触发熔断 ---
            st.error("🚫 安全警报：连续验证失败次数过多，账户已被锁定！")
            AuthService.set_lock_state(username, True)

            audit_logger.critical(
                f"{IMMUTABLE_MARKER} [SECURITY LOCKOUT] User {username} locked due to max auth failures.",
                extra={"user": username, "action": "AUTO_LOCK", "func": "SecurityGate"}
            )

            time.sleep(2)
            SessionManager.logout()

    @staticmethod
    def authorize_action(
            action_key: str,
            ui_key_suffix: str = "",
            require_reason: bool = False,
            help_text: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """
        [主方法] 渲染验证 UI 并返回授权结果
        """
        # 1. 身份预检
        user = SessionManager.get_current_user()
        if not user: return False, ""
        username = user.get("username")

        # 2. 加载策略
        tokens = SecurityPolicyManager.get_required_tokens(action_key)
        meta = SecurityPolicyManager.get_action_metadata(action_key)

        action_name = meta.get("name", action_key)
        description = help_text or meta.get("description", "")

        # 3. 渲染 UI
        st.markdown(f"##### 🔐 安全验证: {action_name}")
        if description: st.caption(description)

        cols_count = len(tokens)
        cols = st.columns(cols_count) if cols_count > 0 else []

        inputs = {}
        unique_ui_key = f"gate_{action_key}_{ui_key_suffix}"

        # [核心] 新版标签映射
        LABEL_MAP = {
            "user": "👤 当前用户密码",
            "query": "👀 数据查询安保码",
            "modify": "✏️ 数据修改安保码",
            "db": "💾 数据库管理码",
            "system": "🛡️ 平台系统管理码"
        }

        for idx, token_type in enumerate(tokens):
            with cols[idx]:
                # 友好提示：如果是多重验证，加序号
                raw_label = LABEL_MAP.get(token_type, f"🔑 {token_type}")
                label = f"{idx + 1}. {raw_label}" if cols_count > 1 else raw_label

                inputs[token_type] = st.text_input(
                    label,
                    type="password",
                    key=f"{unique_ui_key}_pwd_{token_type}"
                )

        reason_text = ""
        if require_reason:
            reason_text = st.text_area(
                "📝 操作备注 (必填)",
                placeholder="请详细说明操作原因，此记录将被永久保存。",
                key=f"{unique_ui_key}_reason"
            )

        # 确认按钮
        if st.button(f" 确认执行", type="primary", use_container_width=True, key=f"{unique_ui_key}_btn"):

            # A. 校验备注
            if require_reason and not reason_text.strip():
                st.error(" 拒绝执行：必须填写操作备注。")
                return False, ""

            # B. 校验密码
            all_valid = True
            failed_token = None

            for token_type, input_val in inputs.items():
                if not SecurityPolicyManager.validate_token(token_type, input_val, username):
                    all_valid = False
                    failed_token = token_type
                    break

            if not all_valid:
                SecurityGate._handle_failure(username, f"{action_key} (Token: {failed_token})")
                return False, ""

            # 验证通过 -> 重置计数器
            if "auth_fail_count" in st.session_state:
                st.session_state["auth_fail_count"] = 0

            # C. 审计记录判定
            # [核心规则] 若 Modify, DB, System 三者都被选中 => 不可删除日志
            required_set = set(tokens)
            critical_set = {"modify", "db", "system"}

            is_immutable = critical_set.issubset(required_set)
            prefix = IMMUTABLE_MARKER if is_immutable else ""

            log_payload = f"{prefix} 授权通过 | Action: {action_key} | Reason: {reason_text}"
            audit_logger.critical(
                log_payload,
                extra={"user": username, "action": "AUTH_GRANT", "func": "SecurityGate"}
            )

            return True, reason_text

        return False, ""
==================== END FILE: ui/components/security.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/components/permission_tree.py ====================
# ui/components/permission_tree.py
"""
文件说明: 权限树渲染组件 (Permission Tree UI Component) - V2.1 Bi-Directional Sync
主要功能:
1. [公有UI类] 递归渲染 Module -> Tab -> Action 的复选框树。
2. [双向联动] 实现 "父选子全选" (向下) 和 "子全选父自动勾" (向上) 的逻辑。
3. [状态管理] 直接操作 st.session_state，保持 UI 响应性。
"""

import streamlit as st
from typing import List, Dict


class PermissionTreeRenderer:

    def __init__(self, user_perms: Dict[str, bool], session_prefix: str = "perm_tree"):
        self.prefix = session_prefix
        self._init_state(user_perms)

    def _get_key(self, node_key: str) -> str:
        """生成唯一的 Session Key"""
        return f"{self.prefix}_{node_key}"

    def _init_state(self, perms: Dict[str, bool]):
        """初始化状态 (仅一次)"""
        if f"{self.prefix}_initialized" not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state[f"{self.prefix}_initialized"] = True
            for k, v in perms.items():
                st.session_state[self._get_key(k)] = v

    def render(self, tree_data: List[Dict]):
        """[主入口] 渲染整棵树"""
        st.markdown("#### 🔒 细粒度权限配置")
        for node in tree_data:
            self._render_node(node, level=0)

    def _render_node(self, node: Dict, level: int):
        """递归渲染节点，包含双向联动逻辑"""
        key = node["key"]
        label = node["name"]
        children = node.get("children", [])
        ui_key = self._get_key(key)

        indent = "&nbsp;" * (level * 4)
        icon = "📦" if level == 0 else ("📑" if level == 1 else "")

        # 1. 确保 Session 中有值 (默认 False)
        if ui_key not in st.session_state:
            st.session_state[ui_key] = False

        # 2. [关键] 向上校正逻辑 (Upward Sync)
        # 在渲染前，检查所有子节点的状态。
        # 如果存在子节点，且所有子节点都被选中，则父节点自动选中；否则取消选中。
        # 注意：这保证了"视觉"上的一致性。
        if children:
            child_keys = [self._get_key(c["key"]) for c in children]
            # 确保子节点 key 在 session 中存在 (防止 key error)
            for k in child_keys:
                if k not in st.session_state: st.session_state[k] = False

            # 计算理论状态
            all_children_checked = all(st.session_state[k] for k in child_keys)

            # 仅当状态不一致时才更新，避免死循环
            if st.session_state[ui_key] != all_children_checked:
                st.session_state[ui_key] = all_children_checked

        # 3. 定义向下传播回调 (Downward Sync)
        def on_change():
            new_val = st.session_state[ui_key]
            self._propagate_down(node, new_val)
            # 这里的改变会在下一次 Rerun 时触发子节点的渲染更新

        # 4. 渲染 Checkbox
        st.checkbox(
            f"{icon} {label}",
            key=ui_key,
            on_change=on_change,
        )

        if node.get("desc"):
            st.caption(f"{indent} └─ {node['desc']}")

        # 5. 递归渲染子节点
        if children:
            with st.container():
                # 物理缩进
                _, col_content = st.columns([0.5 + (level * 0.3), 10])
                with col_content:
                    for child in children:
                        self._render_node(child, level + 1)

    def _propagate_down(self, node: Dict, new_value: bool):
        """[向下联动] 父级改变 -> 递归强制设置所有子孙级"""
        children = node.get("children", [])
        for child in children:
            child_key = self._get_key(child["key"])
            st.session_state[child_key] = new_value
            # 递归处理孙节点
            self._propagate_down(child, new_value)

    def get_selected_keys(self, tree_data: List[Dict]) -> List[str]:
        """获取当前所有被勾选的 Key (用于保存)"""
        selected = []

        def traverse(nodes):
            for n in nodes:
                # 只保存勾选的
                if st.session_state.get(self._get_key(n["key"]), False):
                    selected.append(n["key"])
                traverse(n.get("children", []))

        traverse(tree_data)
        return selected
==================== END FILE: ui/components/permission_tree.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/components/safety.py ====================
# ui/components/safety.py
"""
文件说明: 安全校验组件 (Safety Verification Component)
主要功能:
1. 提供高危操作前的二次确认 UI。
2. 校验当前用户密码或系统运维密码 (DB_OPERATOR_PWD)。
3. 强制输入确认短语 (Confirmation Phrase) 以防止误操作。
"""

import streamlit as st
from typing import Optional, Tuple

from config.settings import settings
from core.services.auth.service import AuthService
from core.sys.context import get_current_user
from core.sys.logger import get_logger

logger = get_logger("SafetyComponent")


def confirm_dangerous_action(
        title: str,
        description: str,
        *,
        confirm_phrase: str = "CONFIRM",
        require_current_password: bool = True,
        require_operator_password: bool = False,
        key_prefix: str = "danger_confirm",
) -> Tuple[bool, Optional[str]]:
    """
    [UI组件] 高危操作统一确认框

    Returns:
        (confirmed: bool, note: str)
    """
    username = get_current_user()

    st.markdown(f"### {title}")
    st.warning(description)

    with st.expander("🛡️ 安全校验 / Security Check", expanded=True):
        # 1. 备注记录
        note = st.text_area(
            "操作备注 (可选):",
            help="建议记录操作原因，例如: '修复数据导入错误'",
            key=f"{key_prefix}_note"
        )

        # 2. 密码校验状态
        current_pwd_ok = True
        operator_pwd_ok = True

        current_pwd_input = ""
        operator_pwd_input = ""

        c1, c2 = st.columns(2)

        with c1:
            if require_current_password:
                current_pwd_input = st.text_input(
                    "👤 验证当前账号密码:",
                    type="password",
                    key=f"{key_prefix}_curr_pwd"
                )
                current_pwd_ok = False  # 默认未通过，等待校验

        with c2:
            if require_operator_password:
                operator_pwd_input = st.text_input(
                    "🔑 验证运维操作密码:",
                    type="password",
                    help="请输入系统配置的 DB_OPERATOR_PWD",
                    key=f"{key_prefix}_op_pwd"
                )
                operator_pwd_ok = False

        # 3. 确认短语
        phrase_input = st.text_input(
            f"✍️ 请输入确认短语: `{confirm_phrase}`",
            key=f"{key_prefix}_phrase"
        )

        if st.button("⚠️ 我已知晓风险，确认执行", type="primary", use_container_width=True, key=f"{key_prefix}_btn"):

            # A. 校验当前用户密码
            if require_current_password:
                if not current_pwd_input:
                    st.error("请输入当前账号密码。")
                    return False, None

                # 使用 AuthService 进行校验 (不改变登录状态)
                # 注意: 这里需要一种不生成 Token 的校验方式，或者复用 authenticate 但忽略结果
                # 为简单起见，我们直接调用 AuthService.authenticate
                ok, _, _ = AuthService.authenticate(username, current_pwd_input)
                if not ok:
                    st.error("当前账号密码错误。")
                    return False, None
                current_pwd_ok = True

            # B. 校验运维密码
            if require_operator_password:
                if operator_pwd_input != settings.DB_OPERATOR_PWD:
                    st.error("运维操作密码错误。")
                    return False, None
                operator_pwd_ok = True

            # C. 校验短语
            if phrase_input != confirm_phrase:
                st.error(f"确认短语不匹配，请输入: {confirm_phrase}")
                return False, None

            # 全部通过
            if current_pwd_ok and operator_pwd_ok:
                logger.info(f"高危操作确认: {title} | User: {username}")
                return True, note

    return False, None
==================== END FILE: ui/components/safety.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/pages/db_data_change.py ====================
# ui/pages/db_data_change.py
"""
文件说明: 数据修改中心 UI (Data Modification Center) - V5.1 Concurrency Safe
主要功能:
1. 库存修改:
   - 单品修改: 使用 'btn_update_single_inv' 策略。
   - 整列删除: 动态选择 'btn_drop_inv_col' (老数据) 或 'btn_drop_inv_col_recent' (新数据)。
2. 资料维护:
   - 批量更新: 使用 'btn_batch_update_cogs' 策略。
   - 新增 SKU: 使用 'btn_create_skus' 策略。
3. [New] 并发锁: 对 Data_Inventory 和 Data_COGS 进行互斥控制。
"""

import streamlit as st
import pandas as pd
import time
import datetime

from core.services.data_manager import DataManager
from ui.components.security import SecurityGate
from core.sys.context import set_current_function
from ui.kernel.session import SessionManager
from core.sys.lock_manager import LockManager  # [New]

# 定义资源键
LOCK_KEY_INV_MOD = "Data_Inventory"
LOCK_KEY_COGS_MOD = "Data_COGS"


def _reset_wizard():
    st.session_state.inv_step = 1
    st.session_state.sel_date = None
    st.session_state.inv_action = None
    st.rerun()


def _init_cogs_data(mgr: DataManager):
    if "cogs_df" not in st.session_state:
        df = mgr.get_cogs_data()
        for col in ["Cost", "Freight", "Cog"]:
            if col in df.columns:
                df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0.0)
        st.session_state.cogs_df = df


def _init_new_sku_df():
    if "new_sku_df" not in st.session_state:
        st.session_state.new_sku_df = pd.DataFrame(
            columns=["SKU", "Category", "SubCategory", "Type", "Cost", "Freight", "Initial_Qty"]
        )


# --- Sub Renderers ---

def _render_inventory_tab(mgr: DataManager, username: str):
    # [New] 锁检查
    can, msg = LockManager.check_access(LOCK_KEY_INV_MOD, username)
    if not can:
        st.error(msg)
        return

    if 'inv_step' not in st.session_state: st.session_state.inv_step = 1
    if 'sel_date' not in st.session_state: st.session_state.sel_date = None
    if 'inv_action' not in st.session_state: st.session_state.inv_action = None

    step = st.session_state.inv_step

    # Step 1
    if step == 1:
        st.markdown("#### Step 1: 选择目标月份")
        cols = mgr.get_inventory_columns()
        if not cols:
            st.warning("暂无库存数据列。")
        else:
            c1, c2 = st.columns([3, 1])
            with c1:
                sel = st.selectbox("请选择库存日期列:", cols)
            with c2:
                st.write("");
                st.write("")
                if st.button("下一步 ➡️", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                    st.session_state.sel_date = sel
                    st.session_state.inv_step = 2
                    st.rerun()

    # Step 2
    elif step == 2:
        target = st.session_state.sel_date
        st.markdown(f"#### Step 2: 选择操作 ({target})")

        c1, c2 = st.columns(2)
        with c1:
            with st.container(border=True):
                st.markdown("##### ✏️ 修改单品库存")
                if st.button("进入修改模式", use_container_width=True):
                    st.session_state.inv_action = "MODIFY"
                    st.session_state.inv_step = 3
                    st.rerun()
        with c2:
            with st.container(border=True):
                st.markdown("##### 🗑️ 删除整列数据")
                st.caption("⚠️ 高危：物理删除该日期列所有数据。")
                if st.button("进入删除模式", type="primary", use_container_width=True):
                    st.session_state.inv_action = "DELETE"
                    st.session_state.inv_step = 3
                    st.rerun()

        st.markdown("---")
        if st.button("⬅️ 返回"): _reset_wizard()

    # Step 3A: Modify
    elif step == 3 and st.session_state.inv_action == "MODIFY":
        target = st.session_state.sel_date
        st.markdown(f"#### Step 3: 修改单品 ({target})")

        skus = mgr.get_all_skus()
        sel_sku = st.selectbox("选择 SKU:", skus)
        curr_val = mgr.get_inventory_value(target, sel_sku)

        c_m1, c_m2 = st.columns(2)
        c_m1.metric("当前库存", curr_val)
        new_v = c_m2.number_input("新库存", value=curr_val, step=1)

        st.markdown("---")
        c1, c2 = st.columns([1, 1])
        with c1:
            if st.button("⬅️ 返回"): st.session_state.inv_step = 2; st.rerun()
        with c2:
            # [Gate] 单品修改
            is_ok, _ = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
                action_key="btn_update_single_inv",
                ui_key_suffix="inv_mod_single",
                require_reason=False
            )
            if is_ok:
                # [New] 加锁
                if LockManager.acquire_lock(LOCK_KEY_INV_MOD, username, f"修改库存:{sel_sku}")[0]:
                    try:
                        success, msg = mgr.update_inventory_qty(target, sel_sku, int(new_v))
                        if success:
                            st.success(msg);
                            time.sleep(1);
                            _reset_wizard()
                        else:
                            st.error(msg)
                    finally:
                        LockManager.release_lock(LOCK_KEY_INV_MOD, username)
                else:
                    st.error("无法获取锁，资源正忙")

    # Step 3B: Delete
    elif step == 3 and st.session_state.inv_action == "DELETE":
        target = st.session_state.sel_date
        st.markdown(f"#### Step 3: 删除整列 ({target})")

        is_old = False
        try:
            t_date = datetime.datetime.strptime(target, "%Y-%m-%d").date()
            if (datetime.date.today() - t_date).days > 30: is_old = True
        except:
            is_old = True

        if is_old:
            gate_key = "btn_drop_inv_col"
            st.error(f"💀 数据已归档超过30天，需 **最高权限验证**。")
        else:
            gate_key = "btn_drop_inv_col_recent"
            st.warning(f"⚠️ 近期数据，需 **当前用户密码**。")

        is_ok, reason = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
            action_key=gate_key,
            ui_key_suffix="inv_del_col",
            require_reason=True
        )

        st.markdown("---")
        if st.button("⬅️ 返回"): st.session_state.inv_step = 2; st.rerun()

        if is_ok:
            # [New] 加锁
            if LockManager.acquire_lock(LOCK_KEY_INV_MOD, username, f"删除列:{target}")[0]:
                try:
                    with st.spinner("Deleting..."):
                        success, msg = mgr.drop_inventory_column(target, reason)
                    if success:
                        st.balloons();
                        st.success(msg);
                        time.sleep(2);
                        _reset_wizard()
                    else:
                        st.error(msg)
                finally:
                    LockManager.release_lock(LOCK_KEY_INV_MOD, username)
            else:
                st.error("无法获取锁")


def _render_cogs_tab(mgr: DataManager, username: str):
    # [New] 锁检查
    can, msg = LockManager.check_access(LOCK_KEY_COGS_MOD, username)
    if not can:
        st.error(msg)
        return

    mode = st.radio("模式选择", ["📝 编辑现有档案", "➕ 批量新增 SKU"], horizontal=True, label_visibility="collapsed")
    st.markdown("---")

    opt_cat = mgr.get_distinct_options("Category")
    opt_sub = mgr.get_distinct_options("SubCategory")
    opt_type = mgr.get_distinct_options("Type")

    # Mode A: Edit
    if "编辑" in mode:
        _init_cogs_data(mgr)
        st.info("💡 说明: 修改 Cost 或 Freight 后，Cog 会自动更新。")

        df_edit = st.session_state.cogs_df
        if not df_edit.empty:
            df_edit["Cog"] = (df_edit["Cost"] + df_edit["Freight"]).round(2)

        edited_df = st.data_editor(
            df_edit,
            key="cogs_editor_smart",
            use_container_width=True,
            num_rows="fixed",
            hide_index=True,
            column_config={
                "SKU": st.column_config.TextColumn("SKU", disabled=True, width="medium"),
                "Cog": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Cog (Total)", disabled=True, format="%.2f"),
                "Cost": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Cost", min_value=0, format="%.2f", required=True),
                "Freight": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Freight", min_value=0, format="%.2f", required=True),
                "Category": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("Category", options=opt_cat),
                "SubCategory": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("SubCategory", options=opt_sub),
                "Type": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("Type", options=opt_type),
                "id": None, "created_at": None, "updated_at": None
            }
        )

        if not edited_df.equals(st.session_state.cogs_df):
            st.session_state.cogs_df = edited_df
            st.rerun()

        st.markdown("---")
        # [Gate] 批量更新
        is_ok, _ = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
            action_key="btn_batch_update_cogs",
            ui_key_suffix="cogs_update",
            require_reason=False
        )

        if is_ok:
            # [New] 加锁
            if LockManager.acquire_lock(LOCK_KEY_COGS_MOD, username, "批量更新COGS")[0]:
                try:
                    success, msg = mgr.update_cogs_smart(edited_df)
                    if success:
                        st.success(msg)
                        del st.session_state.cogs_df
                        time.sleep(2);
                        st.rerun()
                    else:
                        st.error(msg)
                finally:
                    LockManager.release_lock(LOCK_KEY_COGS_MOD, username)
            else:
                st.error("资源忙，请稍后")

    # Mode B: Create
    else:
        _init_new_sku_df()
        st.info("💡 说明: SKU, Cost, Freight 为必填项。Initial_Qty 将写入最新月份库存。")

        df_new = st.session_state.new_sku_df
        for c in ["Cost", "Freight", "Cog", "Initial_Qty"]:
            if c not in df_new.columns: df_new[c] = 0.0

        if not df_new.empty:
            df_new["Cost"] = pd.to_numeric(df_new["Cost"], errors='coerce').fillna(0.0)
            df_new["Freight"] = pd.to_numeric(df_new["Freight"], errors='coerce').fillna(0.0)
            df_new["Cog"] = (df_new["Cost"] + df_new["Freight"]).round(2)

        edited_new = st.data_editor(
            df_new,
            key="cogs_create_new",
            use_container_width=True,
            num_rows="dynamic",
            hide_index=True,
            column_config={
                "SKU": st.column_config.TextColumn("SKU (必填)", required=True),
                "Category": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("Category", options=opt_cat),
                "SubCategory": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("SubCategory", options=opt_sub),
                "Type": st.column_config.SelectboxColumn("Type", options=opt_type),
                "Cost": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Cost", min_value=0, format="%.2f", required=True),
                "Freight": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Freight", min_value=0, format="%.2f", required=True),
                "Cog": st.column_config.NumberColumn("Cog (Auto)", disabled=True, format="%.2f"),
                "Initial_Qty": st.column_config.NumberColumn("当前库存", min_value=0, step=1, format="%d",
                                                             required=True)
            }
        )

        if not edited_new.equals(st.session_state.new_sku_df):
            st.session_state.new_sku_df = edited_new
            st.rerun()

        st.markdown("---")

        # [Gate] 批量新增
        is_ok, _ = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
            action_key="btn_create_skus",
            ui_key_suffix="cogs_create",
            require_reason=False
        )

        if is_ok:
            valid_rows = []
            if not edited_new.empty:
                for _, row in edited_new.iterrows():
                    s = str(row.get("SKU", "")).strip()
                    if s and pd.notna(row.get("Cost")) and pd.notna(row.get("Freight")):
                        valid_rows.append(row.to_dict())

            if not valid_rows:
                st.error(" 没有有效的行 (SKU, Cost, Freight 均为必填)")
            else:
                # [New] 加锁
                if LockManager.acquire_lock(LOCK_KEY_COGS_MOD, username, "批量新增SKU")[0]:
                    try:
                        success, msg = mgr.batch_create_skus(valid_rows)
                        if success:
                            st.success(msg)
                            st.session_state.new_sku_df = pd.DataFrame(columns=edited_new.columns)
                            time.sleep(2);
                            st.rerun()
                        else:
                            st.error(msg)
                    finally:
                        LockManager.release_lock(LOCK_KEY_COGS_MOD, username)
                else:
                    st.error("资源忙")


# --- Main ---
def render():
    set_current_function("数据修改中心")
    st.title("🛠️ 数据修改中心")

    # 获取用户信息用于锁管理
    user_info = SessionManager.get_current_user()
    username = user_info.get("username") if user_info else "Unknown"

    mgr = DataManager()
    tab_inv, tab_cogs = st.tabs(["📦 修改库存", "📝 资料维护"])

    with tab_inv: _render_inventory_tab(mgr, username)
    with tab_cogs: _render_cogs_tab(mgr, username)

# ui/pages/db_admin.py
"""
文件说明: 数据库运维中心 UI (Database Admin Console) - V5.0 Config Driven
主要功能:
1. [Refactor] 全面接入 SecurityGate，基于 Action Key 鉴权。
2. 交互优化: 保持进度条与友好提示。
3. 权限管理: 动作权限由 action_registry.json 统一控制。
"""

import time
import os
import datetime
import streamlit as st
import pandas as pd
from typing import List, Dict, Tuple

from config.settings import settings
from core.services.database_service import DatabaseService
from ui.kernel.session import SessionManager
from ui.components.security import SecurityGate
from core.sys.context import set_current_function


def _build_options_map(files: List[str]) -> Tuple[List[str], Dict[str, str]]:
    options = {}
    for f in files:
        display = DatabaseService.parse_filename_to_display(f)
        if display in options: display += f" ({f})"
        options[display] = f
    return sorted(options.keys(), reverse=True), options


def _simulate_progress(label="Processing...", speed=0.02):
    bar = st.progress(0, text=label)
    for i in range(1, 91):
        time.sleep(speed)
        bar.progress(i, text=label)
    return bar


# --- Tab Renderers ---

def _render_backup_tab(service: DatabaseService):
    st.info("💡 说明：此操作将为当前数据库的所有表创建全量快照 (System Snapshot)。")

    with st.container(border=True):
        c1, c2 = st.columns([3, 1])
        with c1:
            tag = st.text_input("备份备注 (可选)", placeholder="请为备份添加备注, 例如: Before_Update")
        with c2:
            st.write("");
            st.write("")

            # [Gate] 创建备份 (Key: btn_create_backup)
            is_approved, _ = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
                action_key="btn_create_backup",
                ui_key_suffix="backup",
                require_reason=False
            )

            if is_approved:
                bar = _simulate_progress("正在执行全量备份 (Mysqldump)...")
                ok, msg = service.create_backup(tag)
                bar.progress(100, text="备份完成")
                if ok:
                    st.success(msg);
                    time.sleep(1);
                    st.rerun()
                else:
                    st.error(msg)


def _render_restore_tab(service: DatabaseService):
    st.warning("⚠️ **高危警告**：恢复操作将 **完全覆盖** 当前数据库，且不可撤销！")
    files = service.list_backups()
    if not files:
        st.info("暂无可用还原点。")
        return

    labels, file_map = _build_options_map(files)
    sel_label = st.selectbox("请选择恢复时间点:", labels)
    real_file = file_map[sel_label]

    st.divider()

    # [Gate] 恢复数据库 (Key: btn_restore_db)
    is_approved, _ = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
        action_key="btn_restore_db",
        ui_key_suffix="restore",
        require_reason=False,
        help_text="高危操作：请输入最高权限密码组合以解锁恢复按钮。"
    )

    if is_approved:
        bar = st.progress(0.0, text="初始化恢复进程...")

        def update_ui(p):
            val = max(0.0, min(p, 1.0))
            bar.progress(val, text=f"正在写入数据库... {int(val * 100)}%")

        with st.spinner("正在还原数据，请勿关闭页面..."):
            ok, msg = service.restore_backup_with_progress(real_file, update_ui)

        if ok:
            st.balloons();
            st.success(f" 数据库已成功回滚至: {sel_label}")
        else:
            st.error(msg)


def _render_manage_tab(service: DatabaseService):
    files = service.list_backups()
    if not files: st.info("暂无历史备份。"); return

    data = []
    for f in files:
        try:
            path = settings.BACKUP_DIR / f
            size = os.path.getsize(path) / 1024
            display = DatabaseService.parse_filename_to_display(f)
            data.append({"备份快照": display, "文件大小": f"{size:.1f} KB"})
        except:
            pass
    st.dataframe(data, use_container_width=True)

    st.markdown("---")
    st.markdown("#### 🗑️ 删除备份")

    labels, file_map = _build_options_map(files)
    sel_label = st.selectbox("选择要删除的备份:", labels, key="del_sel")
    real_file = file_map[sel_label]

    # [Gate] 删除备份 (Key: btn_delete_backup)
    is_approved, _ = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
        action_key="btn_delete_backup",
        ui_key_suffix="del_backup",
        require_reason=False
    )

    if is_approved:
        bar = _simulate_progress("正在删除...", speed=0.01)
        ok, msg = service.delete_backup(real_file)
        bar.progress(100, text="已删除")
        if ok:
            st.toast(f"已删除: {sel_label}");
            time.sleep(1);
            st.rerun()
        else:
            st.error(msg)


def _render_delete_tab(service: DatabaseService):
    st.error("💀 **极度危险区**：此操作将物理删除数据库中的业务数据，不可逆！")
    with st.container(border=True):
        st.markdown("#### 🧹 按日期区间清洗数据")
        c1, c2 = st.columns(2)
        today = datetime.date.today()
        with c1:
            start_d = st.date_input("起始日期 (含)", value=today, key="d_start")
        with c2:
            end_d = st.date_input("结束日期 (含)", value=today, key="d_end")

        if start_d > end_d: st.error("日期无效"); return

        st.info("受影响范围：\n1. 交易数据 (Transaction)\n2. 报表源数据 (Clean Log)\n3. 库存列 (Inventory Columns)")
        st.markdown("---")

        # [Gate] 数据清洗 (Key: btn_clean_data)
        # 此操作强制要求备注 (require_reason=True)
        is_approved, reason = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
            action_key="btn_clean_data",
            ui_key_suffix="clean_data",
            require_reason=True,
            help_text="请输入最高权限密码并填写原因。"
        )

        if is_approved:
            bar = st.progress(0, text="初始化...")
            try:
                bar.progress(30, text="扫描数据表...")
                time.sleep(0.5)
                bar.progress(60, text="清洗数据列...")

                ok, msg = service.delete_business_data_by_range(start_d, end_d, reason)
                bar.progress(100, text="完成")
                if ok:
                    st.balloons();
                    st.success(" 数据清洗完成")
                    with st.expander("详细报告"):
                        st.text(msg)
                else:
                    st.error(f"失败: {msg}")
            except Exception as e:
                st.error(f"Error: {e}")


# --- Main ---
def render():
    set_current_function("数据库运维")
    st.title("🗄️ 数据库运维中心")

    service = DatabaseService()
    user = SessionManager.get_current_user()
    is_admin = user.get("is_admin", False)
    is_super = (user.get("username") == settings.SUPER_ADMIN_USER)

    if not is_admin: st.error(" 权限不足"); return

    tabs = ["📤 创建备份", "📥 备份恢复", "🗂️ 历史备份管理"]
    if is_super: tabs.append("☢️ 数据删除 (Data Deletion)")

    st_tabs = st.tabs(tabs)

    with st_tabs[0]:
        _render_backup_tab(service)
    with st_tabs[1]:
        _render_restore_tab(service)
    with st_tabs[2]:
        _render_manage_tab(service)
    if len(st_tabs) > 3:
        with st_tabs[3]: _render_delete_tab(service)
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/db_admin.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/pages/audit_logs.py ====================
# ui/pages/audit_logs.py
"""
文件说明: 安全审计日志中心 (Audit Logs) - V5.0 Config Driven Security
主要功能:
1. 多维日志视图 (3 Tabs).
2. [Refactor] 安全升级: 接入 V5 SecurityGate，基于 Action Key 鉴权。
3. 视图模式: 默认脱敏，上帝视角解锁。
4. 特权清洗: 强制备注，自动审计。
"""

import streamlit as st
import datetime
import pandas as pd
from typing import Tuple

from config.settings import settings
from core.services.log_service import LogService
from ui.kernel.session import SessionManager
from ui.styles import StyleManager
from ui.components.security import SecurityGate  # [New]
from core.sys.context import set_current_function
from core.sys.logger import get_logger

app_logger = get_logger("AuditCenter")


# ==============================================================================
# UI 辅助组件
# ==============================================================================
def _render_common_filters(df: pd.DataFrame, key_prefix: str):
    with st.container(border=True):
        c1, c2 = st.columns([1, 2])
        with c1:
            today = datetime.date.today()
            date_range = st.date_input("📅 时间范围", value=(today - datetime.timedelta(days=7), today),
                                       key=f"{key_prefix}_date")
        with c2:
            all_users = sorted(df["user"].unique().tolist()) if "user" in df.columns else []
            selected_users = st.multiselect("👤 用户筛选", all_users, key=f"{key_prefix}_user")
        return date_range, selected_users


def _apply_filters(df: pd.DataFrame, date_range, selected_users) -> pd.DataFrame:
    if df.empty: return df
    if len(date_range) == 2:
        s = date_range[0].strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
        e = (date_range[1] + datetime.timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
        df = df[(df["time"] >= s) & (df["time"] < e)]
    if selected_users:
        df = df[df["user"].isin(selected_users)]
    return df


def _process_display_data(df: pd.DataFrame, is_unmasked: bool) -> pd.DataFrame:
    if df.empty: return df
    df_show = df.copy()
    if not is_unmasked:
        if "message" in df_show.columns:
            df_show["message"] = df_show["message"].apply(
                lambda x: (str(x)[:80] + " ... (🔒 Masked)") if len(str(x)) > 80 else x)
        cols_to_drop = ["raw_msg", "trace", "loc"]
        df_show.drop(columns=[c for c in cols_to_drop if c in df_show.columns], inplace=True)
    return df_show


def _render_purge_zone(filename: str, tab_name: str):
    """[重构] 特权清洗区 - 配置驱动"""
    user = SessionManager.get_current_user()
    if user.get("username") != settings.SUPER_ADMIN_USER: return

    st.markdown("---")
    with st.expander(f"☢️ 特权区域: 清洗 [{tab_name}] 日志", expanded=False):
        st.error("警告：此操作不可逆！将物理删除指定范围内的日志文件。")

        c1, c2 = st.columns(2)
        today = datetime.date.today()
        p_start = c1.date_input("开始日期", value=today, key=f"{tab_name}_ps")
        p_end = c2.date_input("结束日期", value=today, key=f"{tab_name}_pe")

        # [Security Gate V5]
        # Action Key: btn_purge_business / btn_purge_infra / btn_purge_system
        # 具体的密码策略由 action_registry.json 定义 (默认 admin+db+sec)
        action_key = f"btn_purge_{tab_name}"

        is_approved, reason = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
            action_key=action_key,
            ui_key_suffix=tab_name,
            require_reason=True
        )

        if is_approved:
            try:
                dt_s = datetime.datetime.combine(p_start, datetime.time(0, 0))
                dt_e = datetime.datetime.combine(p_end, datetime.time(23, 59))

                count = LogService.purge_logs_by_range(
                    filename, dt_s, dt_e,
                    operator=user.get("username"),
                    reason=reason
                )

                st.success(f" 清洗完成，已删除 {count} 条记录。")
                st.rerun()
            except Exception as e:
                st.error(f"执行失败: {e}")


# ==============================================================================
# Tab Renderers
# ==============================================================================
# (Tab Renderers 逻辑保持简洁，与 V4.0 无大变化，主要复用 LogService)
def render_business_tab(is_unmasked: bool):
    df = LogService.get_logs_as_df("app.log")
    date_range, sel_users = _render_common_filters(df, "app")
    action_filter = st.multiselect(" 动作筛选", df["action"].unique().tolist() if "action" in df.columns else [],
                                   key="app_act")

    df_filtered = _apply_filters(df, date_range, sel_users)
    if action_filter: df_filtered = df_filtered[df_filtered["action"].isin(action_filter)]
    df_display = _process_display_data(df_filtered, is_unmasked)

    st.markdown(f"**共 {len(df_display)} 条记录**")
    cols = ["time", "user", "ip", "func", "action", "message"]
    if is_unmasked and "raw_msg" in df.columns: cols.append("raw_msg")
    cols = [c for c in cols if c in df_display.columns]

    st.dataframe(df_display[cols], use_container_width=True, hide_index=True)
    _render_purge_zone("app.log", "business")  # 注意 key 小写匹配 json


def render_infra_tab(is_unmasked: bool):
    df = LogService.get_logs_as_df("audit.log")
    date_range, sel_users = _render_common_filters(df, "audit")
    sql_acts = st.multiselect(" SQL 动作", ["INSERT", "UPDATE", "DELETE", "TRUNCATE", "SELECT"], key="audit_act")

    df_filtered = _apply_filters(df, date_range, sel_users)
    if sql_acts:
        pat = "|".join(sql_acts)
        df_filtered = df_filtered[df_filtered["action"].astype(str).str.upper().str.contains(pat)]
    df_display = _process_display_data(df_filtered, is_unmasked)

    st.markdown(f"**共 {len(df_display)} 条记录**")
    cols = ["time", "user", "ip", "func", "action", "table", "message"]
    if is_unmasked: cols.append("raw_msg")
    cols = [c for c in cols if c in df_display.columns]
    st.dataframe(df_display[cols], use_container_width=True, hide_index=True)
    _render_purge_zone("audit.log", "infra")


def render_system_tab(is_unmasked: bool):
    df = LogService.get_logs_as_df("error.log")
    if not df.empty and "func" in df.columns:
        st.markdown("#### 📊 故障概览")
        c1, c2, c3 = st.columns(3)
        c1.metric("总报错数", len(df))
        top_module = df["func"].mode()[0] if not df["func"].empty else "-"
        c2.metric("高频模块", top_module)
        c3.metric("最近时间", df.iloc[0]["time"] if not df.empty else "-")
        st.divider()

    date_range, sel_users = _render_common_filters(df, "error")
    all_funcs = df["func"].unique().tolist() if "func" in df.columns else []
    sel_funcs = st.multiselect("🧩 故障功能模块", all_funcs, key="err_func")

    df_filtered = _apply_filters(df, date_range, sel_users)
    if sel_funcs: df_filtered = df_filtered[df_filtered["func"].isin(sel_funcs)]
    df_display = _process_display_data(df_filtered, is_unmasked)

    st.markdown(f"**共 {len(df_display)} 条异常**")
    cols = ["time", "user", "func", "message"]
    if is_unmasked:
        if "trace" in df.columns: cols.append("trace")
        if "loc" in df.columns: cols.append("loc")
    cols = [c for c in cols if c in df_display.columns]
    st.dataframe(df_display[cols], use_container_width=True, hide_index=True)
    _render_purge_zone("error.log", "system")


# ==============================================================================
# Main
# ==============================================================================
def render():
    set_current_function("安全审计日志")
    user = SessionManager.get_current_user()
    if not user.get("is_admin", False): st.error(" 权限不足"); return

    # Top Bar
    c_title, c_tool = st.columns([3, 1])
    with c_title:
        st.title("📜 安全审计日志")

    if "audit_unmasked" not in st.session_state: st.session_state["audit_unmasked"] = False
    current_mode = st.session_state["audit_unmasked"]

    with c_tool:
        st.write("")
        if current_mode:
            StyleManager.apply_unmasked_style()
            if st.button("🔒 隐藏敏感信息", use_container_width=True, type="secondary"):
                st.session_state["audit_unmasked"] = False
                st.rerun()
        else:
            if st.button("🔓 显示完整信息", use_container_width=True, type="primary"):
                st.session_state["show_auth_modal"] = True

    # Unlock Modal
    if st.session_state.get("show_auth_modal", False) and not current_mode:
        with st.container(border=True):
            st.warning("⚠️ 正在请求 [上帝视角]：此操作将展示所有敏感数据，并被记录。")

            # [Security Gate V5]
            # Key: btn_unlock_view (config: admin, db, sec)
            is_approved, _ = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
                action_key="btn_unlock_view",
                require_reason=False
            )

            if st.button(" 取消", use_container_width=True):
                st.session_state["show_auth_modal"] = False
                st.rerun()

            if is_approved:
                st.session_state["audit_unmasked"] = True
                st.session_state["show_auth_modal"] = False
                st.rerun()

    # Tabs
    modules_config = settings.load_modules_config()
    audit_config = next((m for m in modules_config if m['key'] == 'audit'), None)
    if not audit_config: st.error("Audit Config Missing"); return

    visible_tabs = audit_config.get('tabs', [])
    tab_labels = [t['name'] for t in visible_tabs]
    st_tabs = st.tabs(tab_labels)

    for i, t_obj in enumerate(st_tabs):
        key = visible_tabs[i]['key']
        with t_obj:
            if key == "business":
                render_business_tab(current_mode)
            elif key == "infra":
                render_infra_tab(current_mode)
            elif key == "system":
                render_system_tab(current_mode)
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/audit_logs.py ====================

# ui/pages/ai_gemini.py
import streamlit as st
from core.services.chat_service import ChatService

def render():
    st.title("🤖 AI 智能助手")

    # 简单聊天界面

            st.write(m["content"])

    if prompt := st.chat_input("Ask something..."):
        svc.add_message(svc.get_active_session()["id"], "user", prompt)
        st.rerun()
        # 注意: 实际 AI 调用逻辑需对接 Google API，这里仅展示界面框架

==================== START FILE: ui/pages/user_admin/tab_users.py ====================
# ui/pages/user_admin/tab_users.py
"""
子模块: 用户与权限管理 (User & Permission Management) - V5.0 UI Refactor
主要功能:
1. 左侧: 用户列表 + 用户配置 (升降级/锁定/重置) + 注册新用户。
2. 右侧: 细粒度权限树 (独占视图)。
"""
import streamlit as st
import time
from typing import List, Dict

from config.settings import settings
from core.services.auth.service import AuthService
from core.services.security.inventory import SecurityInventory
from core.services.security.policy_manager import SecurityPolicyManager
from ui.components.permission_tree import PermissionTreeRenderer
from ui.components.security import SecurityGate
from core.sys.logger import get_logger

logger = get_logger("UserAdmin")


def _is_super_admin(username):
    return username == settings.SUPER_ADMIN_USER


def _load_user_list():
    df = AuthService.list_users()
    if df.empty: return df

    # [UI] 状态 -> 等级
    def get_level(row):
        if _is_super_admin(row["username"]): return "👑 全站管理员"
        if row["is_locked"]: return "🔴 锁定"
        if row["is_admin"]: return "🛡️ 管理员"
        return "🟢 用户"

    df["等级"] = df.apply(get_level, axis=1)
    return df


def _filter_tree_by_permissions(full_tree: List[Dict], user_perms: Dict[str, bool]) -> List[Dict]:
    filtered_tree = []
    for mod in full_tree:
        mod_key = mod["key"]
        if mod_key == "public" or user_perms.get(mod_key):
            new_mod = mod.copy()
            new_mod["children"] = []
            for tab in mod.get("children", []):
                tab_key = tab["key"]
                if tab_key in user_perms:
                    new_mod["children"].append(tab)
            if new_mod["children"]:
                filtered_tree.append(new_mod)
    return filtered_tree


def render(current_user: str, am_i_super: bool):
    # 布局调整: 左侧稍微窄一点，右侧宽一点给权限树
    c1, c2 = st.columns([1.5, 2.5])

    # 权限与职能检查
    my_perms = {}
    if not am_i_super:
        my_perms = AuthService.get_permissions(current_user)

    can_create = am_i_super or SecurityPolicyManager.get_admin_capability("can_create_user")
    can_lock = am_i_super or SecurityPolicyManager.get_admin_capability("can_lock_user")
    can_reset = am_i_super or SecurityPolicyManager.get_admin_capability("can_reset_pwd")
    can_manage_perms = am_i_super or SecurityPolicyManager.get_admin_capability("can_manage_perms")

    # =========================================================================
    # 左侧: 列表 & 基础配置
    # =========================================================================
    with c1:
        st.subheader("👥 用户名录")
        df_users = _load_user_list()

        # 1. 用户选择器
        selected_user = st.selectbox(
            "👉 选择操作对象:",
            df_users["username"].tolist() if not df_users.empty else [],
            key="ua_user_select"
        )

        # 2. 用户表格
        if not df_users.empty:
            # 只显示核心列
            st.dataframe(
                df_users[["username", "等级"]],
                use_container_width=True,
                hide_index=True
            )

        st.write("")  # Spacer

        # 3. 配置区域 (折叠框，移动至此)
        if selected_user:
            target_info = df_users[df_users["username"] == selected_user].iloc[0]
            t_is_super = _is_super_admin(selected_user)
            t_is_admin = target_info["is_admin"]
            t_is_locked = target_info["is_locked"]

            # 状态重置: 切换用户时清理 Tree 状态
            if st.session_state.get("last_ua_user") != selected_user:
                keys_to_del = [k for k in st.session_state.keys() if k.startswith("ptree_")]
                for k in keys_to_del: del st.session_state[k]
                st.session_state["last_ua_user"] = selected_user
                st.rerun()

            with st.expander(f"⚙️ 配置: {selected_user}", expanded=True):
                # A. 信息概览
                mc1, mc2 = st.columns(2)
                mc1.metric("失败次数", target_info["failed_attempts"])
                mc2.metric("当前状态", "🔴 锁定" if t_is_locked else "🟢 正常")

                st.divider()

                # B. 角色升降级 (仅 Super)
                if am_i_super:
                    if t_is_super:
                        st.info("🔒 无法变更全站管理员角色")
                    else:
                        rc1, rc2 = st.columns([1, 1])
                        with rc1:
                            if t_is_admin:
                                if st.button("⬇️ 降级为用户", use_container_width=True):
                                    from core.components.db.client import DBClient
                                    DBClient.execute_stmt("UPDATE User_Account SET is_admin=0 WHERE username=:u",
                                                          {"u": selected_user})
                                    st.success("已降级");
                                    time.sleep(0.5);
                                    st.rerun()
                            else:
                                st.write("")  # 占位
                        with rc2:
                            if not t_is_admin:
                                if st.button("⬆️ 升级为管理员", use_container_width=True):
                                    from core.components.db.client import DBClient
                                    DBClient.execute_stmt("UPDATE User_Account SET is_admin=1 WHERE username=:u",
                                                          {"u": selected_user})
                                    st.success("已升级");
                                    time.sleep(0.5);
                                    st.rerun()
                            else:
                                st.write("")  # 占位
                    st.divider()

                # C. 锁定/解锁
                if can_lock and not t_is_super:
                    lc1, lc2 = st.columns(2)
                    if t_is_locked:
                        with lc1:
                            # [Gate] 解锁
                            if SecurityGate.authorize_action("btn_unlock_user", "unlock", help_text="解锁账号")[0]:
                                AuthService.set_lock_state(selected_user, False)
                                logger.info(f"解锁: {selected_user}", extra={"action": "UNLOCK", "user": current_user})
                                st.rerun()
                    else:
                        with lc2:
                            # [Gate] 锁定
                            if SecurityGate.authorize_action("btn_lock_user", "lock", help_text="锁定账号")[0]:
                                AuthService.set_lock_state(selected_user, True)
                                logger.warning(f"锁定: {selected_user}", extra={"action": "LOCK", "user": current_user})
                                st.rerun()
                    st.divider()

                # D. 重置密码
                if can_reset and not t_is_super:
                    new_pwd_reset = st.text_input("重置密码", type="password", placeholder="输入新密码",
                                                  key="reset_val")
                    if SecurityGate.authorize_action("btn_reset_pwd", "reset_pwd")[0]:
                        if new_pwd_reset:
                            AuthService.reset_password(selected_user, new_pwd_reset)
                            st.success("密码已重置")
                        else:
                            st.error("密码为空")

        # 4. 注册新用户 (折叠框，放在最下)
        st.write("")
        if can_create:
            with st.expander("➕ 注册新用户", expanded=False):
                new_u = st.text_input("用户名", key="new_u")
                new_p = st.text_input("密码", type="password", key="new_p")
                is_adm = st.checkbox("设为管理员", key="new_is_adm") if am_i_super else False

                # [Gate] 注册
                is_ok, _ = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
                    action_key="btn_create_user",
                    ui_key_suffix="create_user",
                    require_reason=False
                )

                if is_ok:
                    if new_u and new_p:
                        ok, msg = AuthService.create_user(new_u, new_p, is_adm)
                        if ok:
                            st.success("创建成功"); time.sleep(1); st.rerun()
                        else:
                            st.error(msg)
                    else:
                        st.error("请填写完整")

    # =========================================================================
    # 右侧: 细粒度权限配置 (独占)
    # =========================================================================
    with c2:
        if not selected_user: return

        # 重新加载状态判断
        # 注意: 这里不需要再读 df_users，直接用 selected_user 查权限即可
        # 但为了获取 is_super/is_admin 属性，上面已经查过了 target_info

        if t_is_super:
            st.info("👑 全站管理员拥有系统所有权限，无需配置细粒度权限。")
            st.caption("如需修改其密码策略，请前往 [密码功能管理] Tab。")

        elif t_is_admin and not am_i_super:
            st.warning("🛡️ 您无法修改其他管理员的权限配置。")

        elif not can_manage_perms:
            st.warning("🚫 您当前的职能设定不允许配置用户权限。")

        else:
            # --- 权限树渲染区 ---
            # [Fix] 移除了多余的 "#### 权限明细" 标题，直接由 Renderer 渲染

            full_tree = SecurityInventory.get_full_permission_tree()

            # 边界过滤: 如果我不是 Super，只能看到我有权分配的模块
            if not am_i_super:
                display_tree = _filter_tree_by_permissions(full_tree, my_perms)
                st.info("️ 仅显示您拥有的权限模块 (权限边界限制)。")
            else:
                display_tree = full_tree

            # 获取目标用户当前权限
            target_perms = AuthService.get_permissions(selected_user)

            # 渲染组件
            renderer = PermissionTreeRenderer(target_perms, session_prefix="ptree")
            renderer.render(display_tree)

            st.markdown("---")

            # [Gate] 保存权限
            is_ok_perm, _ = SecurityGate.authorize_action(
                action_key="btn_update_perms",
                ui_key_suffix="save_perms",
                require_reason=False
            )

            if is_ok_perm:
                selected_keys = renderer.get_selected_keys(display_tree)
                perms_map = {k: True for k in selected_keys}

                # 增量更新逻辑
                if not am_i_super:
                    visible_keys = []

                    def extract_keys(nodes):
                        for n in nodes:
                            visible_keys.append(n["key"])
                            extract_keys(n.get("children", []))

                    extract_keys(display_tree)

                    final_perms = target_perms.copy()
                    for vk in visible_keys:
                        if vk in perms_map:
                            final_perms[vk] = True
                        else:
                            if vk in final_perms: del final_perms[vk]
                    AuthService.set_permissions(selected_user, final_perms)
                else:
                    AuthService.set_permissions(selected_user, perms_map)

                logger.info(f"权限更新: {selected_user}", extra={"action": "UPDATE_PERMS", "user": current_user})
                st.success("权限已保存！")
                time.sleep(1);
                st.rerun()
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/user_admin/tab_users.py ====================


==================== START FILE: ui/pages/user_admin/tab_policies.py ====================
# ui/pages/user_admin/tab_policies.py
"""
子模块: 密码功能管理 (Security Policy Management) - V2.2 Final Fix
主要功能:
1. 全站管理员在此配置每个动作需要验证的密码组合。
2. 支持 User/Query/Modify/DB/System 五种安全级别。
"""
import streamlit as st
import time
from core.services.security.inventory import SecurityInventory
from core.services.security.policy_manager import SecurityPolicyManager


def render():
    """渲染入口函数"""
    st.info("💡在此配置全站每个关键动作的密码验证等级。更改即时生效。")

    # 获取所有动作
    actions = SecurityInventory.get_flat_action_list()

    # [核心] 定义可选的安全令牌
    TOKEN_OPTIONS = ["user", "query", "modify", "db", "system"]

    TOKEN_LABELS = {
        "user": "当前用户密码",
        "query": "L1-查询安保码",
        "modify": "L2-修改安保码",
        "db": "L3-数据库管理码",
        "system": "L4-系统管理码"
    }

    with st.container(border=True):
        st.markdown(f"**共 {len(actions)} 个受控动作点**")
        # 按模块分组
        modules = sorted(list(set(a["module_name"] for a in actions if a["module_name"])))

        for mod in modules:
            with st.expander(f"📦 {mod}", expanded=False):
                mod_actions = [a for a in actions if a["module_name"] == mod]
                for act in mod_actions:
                    c1, c2 = st.columns([2, 3])
                    key = act["key"]
                    name = act["name"]

                    # 获取当前策略 (优先 Override)
                    current_tokens = SecurityPolicyManager.get_required_tokens(key)

                    with c1:
                        st.markdown(f"**{name}**")
                        st.caption(f"ID: `{key}`")
                        if act.get("description"):
                            st.caption(f"📝 {act['description']}")

                    with c2:
                        new_tokens = st.multiselect(
                            "验证要求",
                            options=TOKEN_OPTIONS,
                            default=current_tokens,
                            key=f"pol_{key}",
                            format_func=lambda x: TOKEN_LABELS.get(x, x.upper())
                        )

                        # 检查变更
                        if set(new_tokens) != set(current_tokens):
                            if st.button("💾 更新策略", key=f"save_{key}"):
                                SecurityPolicyManager.save_policy_override(key, new_tokens)
                                st.toast(f"策略已更新: {name}")
                                time.sleep(0.5);
                                st.rerun()
                    st.divider()
==================== END FILE: ui/pages/user_admin/tab_policies.py ====================

# ui/pages/user_admin/__init__.py
"""
文件说明: 用户与权限管理入口 (User Admin Entry)
主要功能:
1. 调度 Tab 子模块。
2. 权限判断与上下文设置。
"""

import streamlit as st
from config.settings import settings
from ui.kernel.session import SessionManager
from core.sys.context import set_current_function

# 导入子模块
from . import tab_users
from . import tab_policies
from . import tab_functions


def _is_super_admin(username):
    return username == settings.SUPER_ADMIN_USER


def render():
    set_current_function("用户权限管理")
    st.title("👤 用户与权限管理中心")

    user = SessionManager.get_current_user()
    if not user:
        st.error("请先登录")
        return

    username = user.get("username")
    is_super = _is_super_admin(username)

    # 定义 Tabs
    tabs = ["👥 用户与权限配置"]
    if is_super:
        tabs.append("🔐 密码功能管理")
        tabs.append("🛡️ 职能管理")

    st_tabs = st.tabs(tabs)

    # Tab 1: 用户管理 (所有人可见，内部有权限控制)
    with st_tabs[0]:
        tab_users.render(username, is_super)

    # Tab 2: 密码策略 (仅 Super)
    if is_super and len(st_tabs) > 1:
        with st_tabs[1]:
            tab_policies.render()

    # Tab 3: 职能管理 (仅 Super)
    if is_super and len(st_tabs) > 2:
        with st_tabs[2]:
            tab_functions.render()
